$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / Arrays1

::Arrays Level 1 #000::
What are the contents of the array after the following statements?
<pre>int bar[4] = \{8, 6, 5, 4\};
int temp;
temp = bar[3];
bar[3] = bar[0];
bar[0] = temp;</pre>
	{
	=\{4, 6, 5, 8\}
	~\{8, 6, 5, 4\}
	~\{6, 5, 5, 4\}
	~\{8, 5, 6, 4\}
	~\{6, 8, 5, 4\}
	}

	}

<pre>int matrix[4] = \{2, 1, 10, 5\};
int temp;
temp = matrix[1];
matrix[1] = matrix[3];
matrix[3] = temp;</pre>
	{
	=\{2, 5, 10, 1\}
	~\{2, 1, 10, 5\}
	~\{2, 1, 2, 5\}
	~\{13, 1, 2, 5\}
	~\{10, 1, 2, 5\}
	}

::Arrays Level 3 #667::

	~9 8 6

int bar[4] = \{6, 7, 7, 2\};
for (int i = 0; i < 3; i = i + 1)
\{
	cout << bar[i] << " ";
\}
	{
	=6 7 7 
	~7 7 2 
	~2 6 9 
	~2 6 7 
	~Run-time error due to out of bound index.
	}
